0"></path><path d="M19.98 10.023c0 .2-.058.399-.168.547l-4.996 7.492a.987.987 0 01-.828.454h-3c-.547 0-.996-.453-.996-1 0-.2.059-.403.168-.551l4.625-6.942-4.625-6.945a.939.939 0 01-.168-.55 1 1 0 01.996-.997h3c.348 0 .649.18.828.45l4.996 7.492c.11.148.168.347.168.55zm0 0"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></aside><main class="docMainContainer_TBSr"><div class="container padding-top--md padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_z5aJ"><div class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/manage-collections"><span>How-to: Manage collections</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Collection operations (CRUD)</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Basic collection operations</h1></header><p>Every object in Weaviate belongs to exactly one collection. Use the examples on this page to manage your collections.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>Terminology</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Newer Weaviate documentation discuses &quot;collections.&quot; Older Weaviate documentation refers to &quot;classes&quot; instead. Expect to see both terms throughout the documentation.</p></div></div>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Python and JS/TS client - Vectorizer Configuration API Changes</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Starting with Weaviate Python client <code>v4.16.0</code>, the <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python#vectorizer-api-changes-v4160">vectorizer configuration API has been updated</a>.<br>
<!-- -->Starting with Weaviate JS/TS client <code>v3.8.0</code>, the <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/typescript#vectorizer-api-changes-v380">vectorizer configuration API has been updated</a>.</p><p>Action required: <strong>Update to the latest client version</strong> and migrate your code to use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/vector-config#specify-a-vectorizer">new vectorizer configuration API</a>.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-a-collection">Create a collection<a href="#create-a-collection" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create a collection" title="Direct link to Create a collection" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>To create a collection, specify at least the collection name. If you don&#x27;t specify any properties, <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#auto-schema"><code>auto-schema</code></a> creates them.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-note admonition_xJq3 alert alert--secondary"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.3 5.69a.942.942 0 0 1-.28-.7c0-.28.09-.52.28-.7.19-.18.42-.28.7-.28.28 0 .52.09.7.28.18.19.28.42.28.7 0 .28-.09.52-.28.7a1 1 0 0 1-.7.3c-.28 0-.52-.11-.7-.3zM8 7.99c-.02-.25-.11-.48-.31-.69-.2-.19-.42-.3-.69-.31H6c-.27.02-.48.13-.69.31-.2.2-.3.44-.31.69h1v3c.02.27.11.5.31.69.2.2.42.31.69.31h1c.27 0 .48-.11.69-.31.2-.19.3-.42.31-.69H8V7.98v.01zM7 2.3c-3.14 0-5.7 2.54-5.7 5.68 0 3.14 2.56 5.7 5.7 5.7s5.7-2.55 5.7-5.7c0-3.15-2.56-5.69-5.7-5.69v.01zM7 .98c3.86 0 7 3.14 7 7s-3.14 7-7 7-7-3.12-7-7 3.14-7 7-7z"></path></svg></span>Capitalization</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Weaviate follows GraphQL naming conventions.</p><ul>
<li class="">Start collection names with an upper case letter.</li>
<li class="">Start property names with a lower case letter.</li>
</ul><p>If you use an initial upper case letter to define a property name, Weaviate changes it to a lower case letter internally.</p></div></div>

<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Production ready collections</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><ul>
<li class=""><strong>Manually define you data schema</strong>:
Avoid using the <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#auto-schema"><code>auto-schema</code></a> feature, instead, manually <a href="#create-a-collection-and-define-properties" class="">define the properties for your collection</a>.</li>
<li class=""><strong>Avoid creating too many collections</strong>:
Using too many collections can lead to scalability issues like high memory usage and degraded query performance. Instead, consider <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/multi-tenancy">using multi-tenancy</a>, where a single collection is subdivided into multiple tenants. For more details, see <a class="" href="/weaviate/starter-guides/managing-collections/collections-scaling-limits">Starter Guides: Scaling limits with collections</a>.</li>
</ul></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-a-collection-and-define-properties">Create a collection and define properties<a href="#create-a-collection-and-define-properties" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create a collection and define properties" title="Direct link to Create a collection and define properties" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Properties are the data fields in your collection. Each property has a name and a data type.</p>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary><p>Additional information</p></summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>Use properties to configure additional parameters such as data type, index characteristics, or tokenization.</p><p>For details, see:</p><ul>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections">References: Configuration: Schema</a></li>
<li class="">
<a href="/weaviate/api/rest\#tag/schema"><p>API References: REST: Schema</p></a>
</li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/datatypes">Available data types</a></li>
</ul></div></div></details>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-a-collection-with-a-vectorizer">Create a collection with a vectorizer<a href="#create-a-collection-with-a-vectorizer" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create a collection with a vectorizer" title="Direct link to Create a collection with a vectorizer" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Specify a <code>vectorizer</code> for a collection that will generate vector embeddings when creating objects and executing vector search queries.</p>

<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Vectorizer configuration</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Find out more about the vectorizer and vector index configuration in <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/vector-config">Manage collections: Vectorizer and vector index</a>.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="disable-auto-schema">Disable auto-schema<a href="#disable-auto-schema" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Disable auto-schema" title="Direct link to Disable auto-schema" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>By default, Weaviate creates missing collections and missing properties. When you configure collections manually, you have more precise control of the collection settings.</p>
<p>To disable <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#auto-schema"><code>auto-schema</code></a> set <code>AUTOSCHEMA_ENABLED: &#x27;false&#x27;</code> in your system configuration file.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="check-if-a-collection-exists">Check if a collection exists<a href="#check-if-a-collection-exists" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Check if a collection exists" title="Direct link to Check if a collection exists" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Get a boolean indicating whether a given collection exists.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="read-a-single-collection-definition">Read a single collection definition<a href="#read-a-single-collection-definition" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Read a single collection definition" title="Direct link to Read a single collection definition" translate="no">​</a></h2>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Sample configuration: Text objects</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>This configuration for text objects defines the following:</p><ul>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Sample configuration: Nested objects</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.22</code></div></div><p>This configuration for nested objects defines the following:</p><ul>
<li class="">
<p>The collection name (<code>Person</code>)</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>The vectorizer module (<code>text2vec-huggingface</code>)</p>
</li>
<li class="">

<li class=""><code>address</code> has <code>object</code> data type</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>The <code>address</code> property has two nested properties (<code>street</code> and <code>city</code>)</p>
</li>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Sample configuration: Generative search</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>This configuration for <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/generative">retrieval augmented generation</a> defines the following:</p><ul>
<li class="">The collection name (<code>Article</code>)</li>
<li class="">The default vectorizer module (<code>text2vec-openai</code>)</li>
<li class="">The generative module (<code>generative-openai</code>)</li>

<li class="">The tokenization option for the <code>url</code> property</li>

<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Sample configuration: Images</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>This configuration for image search defines the following:</p><ul>
<li class="">
<p>The collection name (<code>Image</code>)</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>The vectorizer module (<code>img2vec-neural</code>)</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>image</code> property configures collection to store image data.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>The vector index distance metric (<code>cosine</code>)</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>A set of properties (<code>image</code>), with the <code>image</code> property set as <code>blob</code>.</p>
</li>
</ul><p>For image searches, see <a class="" href="/weaviate/search/image">Image search</a>.</p><div class="language-json codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="read-all-collection-definitions">Read all collection definitions<a href="#read-all-collection-definitions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Read all collection definitions" title="Direct link to Read all collection definitions" translate="no">​</a></h2>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="update-a-collection-definition">Update a collection definition<a href="#update-a-collection-definition" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Update a collection definition" title="Direct link to Update a collection definition" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Replication factor change</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>The replication factor of a collection cannot be updated by updating the collection&#x27;s definition.</p><p>From <code>v1.32</code> by using <a class="" href="/deploy/configuration/replica-movement">replica movement</a>, the <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#replication">replication factor</a> of a shard can be changed.</p></div></div>
<p>You can update a collection definition to change the <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#mutability">mutable collection settings</a>.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="delete-a-collection">Delete a collection<a href="#delete-a-collection" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Delete a collection" title="Direct link to Delete a collection" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<p>You can delete any unwanted collection(s), along with the data that they contain.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-caution admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Deleting a collection also deletes its objects</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>When you <strong>delete a collection, you delete all associated objects</strong>!</p><p>Be very careful with deletes on a production database and anywhere else that you have important data.</p></div></div>
<p>This code deletes a collection and its objects.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="curl">Curl</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="add-a-property">Add a property<a href="#add-a-property" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Add a property" title="Direct link to Add a property" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary><p>Indexing limitations after data import</p></summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>There are no index limitations when you add collection properties before you import data.</p><p>If you add a new property after you import data, there is an impact on indexing.<br><br></p><p>Property indexes are built at import time. If you add a new property after importing some data, pre-existing objects index aren&#x27;t automatically updated to add the new property. This means pre-existing objects aren&#x27;t added to the new property index. Queries may return unexpected results because the index only includes new objects.<br><br></p><p>To create an index that includes all of the objects in a collection, do one of the following:</p><ul>
<li class="">New collections: Add all of the collection&#x27;s properties before importing objects.</li>
<li class="">Existing collections: Export the existing data from the collection. Re-create it with the new property. Import the data into the updated collection.</li>
</ul><p>We are working on a re-indexing API to allow you to re-index the data after adding a property. This will be available in a future release.</p></div></div></details>
